mame2010 per-game video output color format and copy status
======================================================================

WHAT THIS DESCRIBES
----------------------------------------------------------------------
mame2010 renders every frame through the software rasterizer
(rgb888/rgb565_draw_primitives), which samples the emulated screen's
bitmap as a texture and writes the visible frame into the output buffer.
This list classifies, per game, the screen's bitmap format - which fixes
what the rasterizer (or a single-screen-quad blit fast path) must do to
produce one output pixel - and the screen orientation, which determines
whether a rotate/flip is also required.

Output buffer format is fixed by the build: XRGB8888 by default, RGB565
under -DM16B. The columns below assume the default XRGB8888 build.

SCREEN FORMAT (MDRV_SCREEN_FORMAT, resolved through MDRV_IMPORT_FROM)
----------------------------------------------------------------------
  BITMAP_FORMAT_INDEXED16 -> paletted   : stores palette INDICES; an
                                          index->RGB lookup is mandatory
                                          emulation work, not a copy.
  BITMAP_FORMAT_RGB32     -> 32bpp direct: same width as the output, so
                                          only a copy (+rotate) is needed.
  BITMAP_FORMAT_RGB15     -> 15bpp direct: 0RGB1555 expanded to 8888.

COPY STATUS (third column = orientation, fourth = rasterizer work)
----------------------------------------------------------------------
  DIRECT32                RGB32 upright: a straight per-row copy; the
                          single-screen-quad fast path can blit it.
  DIRECT32+ROT            RGB32 rotated/flipped: copy with a rotate pass
                          (the frontend can take ROT instead).
  CONVERT(pal->8888)      paletted: palette index->RGB lookup, mandatory.
  CONVERT(1555->8888)     15bpp expanded one pixel at a time.
  +ROT suffix             a rotate/flip is also required.

SUMMARY (of 8892 games)
----------------------------------------------------------------------
  paletted (index->RGB) .........  6861
  RGB32 direct ..................  1648
  RGB15 direct ..................   186
  no screen / unresolved ........   197
